<Dataviews xmlns="http://cdaweb.gsfc.nasa.gov/schema">
  <DataviewDescription>
    <Id>sp_phys</Id>
    <EndpointAddress>https://cdaweb.gsfc.nasa.gov/WS/cdasr/1/dataviews/sp_phys</EndpointAddress>
    <Title>CDAWeb (Space Physics Public Data)</Title>
    <Subtitle>CDAWeb contains selected public non-solar heliophysics data from current and past heliophysics missions and projects.  Many datasets from current missions are updated regularly (even daily), including reprocessing older time periods, and SPDF only preserves the latest version.  To find all of the public data and documents archived by the SPDF, see &lt;a href="https://spdf.gsfc.nasa.gov/pub"&gt;the SPDF archive&lt;/a&gt;. To search for additional heliophysics data products, check &lt;a href="https://heliophysicsdata.gsfc.nasa.gov"&gt;the heliophysics data portal&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;P&gt;&lt;P&gt; &lt;font color="Blue"&gt;REMINDER: CDAWeb offers CREATION of subset/supersets of data sets (by date and variables), CREATION of uniformly time binned data, PLOTS in PDF, PS and PNG formatted files, MOVIES of specific image sequences, ON-THE-FLY Inventory plots, ADJUSTABLE height time/spectrogram plots, plus many more options...&lt;/font&gt;</Subtitle>
    <UnderConstruction>false</UnderConstruction>
    <NoticeUrl>//cdaweb.gsfc.nasa.gov/notices.html</NoticeUrl>
    <PublicAccess>true</PublicAccess>
  </DataviewDescription>
</Dataviews>
